 apane bhaashan main raman singh ne chhattisgarh kii janata ko bataaya ki kis tarah se unki sarkaar rajya ko vikaas ke path par lekar ai he
 He claimed prosperity in the state and also said that the state of Chhattisgarh is free from intruders
 manch se utaarte hi mukhyamantri raman singh ne TMC or mamata banerjee par nishaanaa saadhaa
 In his statement, Raman Singh also attacked the Congress
 unhone khuletaur par kaha ki jo baahar se aae hai unhen khadeda janaa chahie
 Raman Singh also referred to the eight-year-old agitation to expel the infiltrators in Assam
 assam main NRC kaa doosraa draft jari hone ke baad se puraa maamla garmaya hua he
 It is being speculated that Chief Minister Raman Singh has made strong remarks about NRC only after the instructions of BJP high command
 laal batti ke istemaal par supreme court ne bada aadesh diya he
 The Supreme Court said that only those sitting in constitutional post will get red light
 iske alaava police, ambulance or anya apaat seva ko neeli batti kaa istemaal karnaa hoga
 The Supreme Court has given three months time to the Center and all the state governments to implement its decision
 supreme court ne kaha he ki rajya sarkarein laal batti kaa istemaal karne vaale logon kii list nahin badha sakati
 According to the order of the Supreme Court, now sirens will be used only in emergency service
 uski bhi aawaaj aisi honi chahie jisase logon ko pareshaani na ho
 The Supreme Court has asked the central and state governments that if they have taken some more decisions regarding the use of red lights, they should be told to the court within three months
 aapako bataa den ki ek puraane aadesh main supreme court ne kaha tha ki viipi gadiyon main laal batti or syran se british raaj kii jhalak milti he
 When Home Minister p Chidambaram refused this facility, then why are these facilities being given to ministers, bureaucrats and other leaders? kendriya samskruti mantri mahesh sharma ne kaha ki divangat purv raashtrapati apije abdul kalam musalmaan hone ke 'baavjood' ek mahaan rashtravaadi the
 His statement has sparked a new controversy
 sharma kaa bayaan nehru smarak sangrahalay or pustkaalay (enemmal) ke nideshak mahesh rangarajan ke istife se paidaa hue vivaad kii prishthbhumi main aayaa he
 The Congress alleges that Rangarajan resigned due to unbearable pressure from the government
 tippaniyan Union Minister Sharma recently talked about freeing the country from 'cultural pollution' and teaching Mahabharata and Ramayana to the students
 kendriya mantri ne ek samachar channel se kaha, 'hamane aurangzeb road kaa naam badalakar ek aise vyakti ke naam par kar diya jo ek muslim hote hue bhi mahaan rashtravaadi the
 ' aapako bataa den ki nai dilli nagarpalika parishad (endiemasi) ne 28 agast ko lutiyans dilli main sthit aurangzeb road kaa naam badalakar apije abdul kalam road karne kii manjuuri di thi
 Sharma's statement comes against the backdrop of the controversy arising out of the resignation of Mahesh Rangarajan, director of the Nehru Memorial Museum and Library (NMML)
 congress kaa aarope he ki sarkaar kii ore se asahneeya dabaav kii vajah se rangarajan ne istipha diya
 The comments kendriya mantri sharma ne haal hi main desh ko 'saanskrithik pradooshan' se mukt karaane or vidhyaarthiyon ko mahabharat tathaa ramayana padhaane kii baat kahi thi
 The Union Minister told a news channel, 'we changed the name of Aurangzeb Road to a person who, despite being a Muslim, was a great nationalist
 ' Let us tell you that on 28 August, the New Delhi Municipal Council (NDMC) approved the renaming of Aurangzeb Road located in Lutyens' Delhi to APJ Abdul Kalam Road
 kendriya mantri sharma ne haal hi main desh ko 'saanskrithik pradooshan' se mukt karaane or vidhyaarthiyon ko mahabharat tathaa ramayana padhaane kii baat kahi thi

 The Bharatiya Janata Party (BJP) has demanded the Prime Minister's resignation after news published about the purchase of mps during a 2008 motion of confidence in a newspaper based on the revelations of the website wikileaks
 loksabhaa main guuruuvaar ko kaarysthan prastaav par charchaa ke dauraan vipaksh kii netaa sushamaa swaraj ne kaha, "samachar patr da hindu main vikiliks ke khulaase ke aadhaar par achambhit karne vaale samachar chap rahe the lekin aaj jo khabar chhapi he vah sharmasaar or kalankit karne vaali he
 "he said that during the motion of confidence, his party had presented proof of the purchase of mps in the House when it was declared a crime but the revelations that have taken place today is not a crime?" They were trying to bring the truth to the people, but in the dark of night, a deal was made to buy mps secretly, is it not a crime? unhone kaha ki haal ke dinon main sarkaar par kaaphi chotein padi hai, lekin is baar us par jo hathaudaa padaa he vah sharmasaar karne vaala he
 He demanded Prime Minister Manmohan Singh to come to the House immediately and announce his resignation and said that now this government does not have the moral right to remain in power even for a minute
 udhar, isse pehle rajyasabha main vipaksh ke netaa arun jetali ne sarkaar par 'raajnneetik or naitik paap' karne kaa aarope lagaate hue kaha ki sarkaar ko turant istipha dena chahie
 According to a report published in the newspaper The Hindu based on the revelations of wikileaks, the purchase of mps through the US Embassy in New Delhi to ensure the government's victory on the confidence motion tabled in Parliament on the nuclear deal with the US in 2008
 50 to 60 crores was spent
 french vikali 'charlie abdo' par hue aatanki hamale menvanted koushi brosake bare main america suraksha agenciyon ne daawa kiya he ki ye donon yues kii 'no fli' list main shaamil the
 32-year-old Sheriff Cowshi and her 34-year-old brother Saad Cowshi had been on the N10 Terror Suspects list for several years by US agencies
 in donon ke bare main america agenciyon ke paas pukhta jaankaree thi, isliye inke naam epabiai ke terririst screening centre ko bheje gaye the
 The Cowshee brothers were then included among the 47,000 people on the 'no fly' list, who were severely restricted from boarding aircraft inside or outside the US
 haalanki, abhi tak america agenciyon ne yah nahin bataaya he ki in donon bhaaiyon ke bare main unhen aisi kya jaankaree mili thi, jiske baad inhen 'no fli' list main shaamil kiya gaya tha
 One of the Cowshee brothers knew quite a bit about France
 yahaan tak ki sheriff koushi ko 2005 kii shuruyaat main giraftaar kiya gaya tha
 The matter was also associated with terror at that time
 2008 main sheriff par cese bhi chalaa tha or us vakt usne sweekaar kiya tha ki vah kattarpanthi he
 The sheriff blamed the US atrocities on inmates in Abu Gareb prison for turning to radicalism
 abu gareb or guantnamo jail main kaidiyon ko third degree ko lekar kaaphi khabaren saamne ai hai

 baharhaal, is maamle main sheriff ko teen saal kii sajaa sunai thi, lekin vah sunwaayee ke dauraan kaaphi samay jail main bitaa chukaa tha, jisaki vajah se vah jaldi hi reeha ho gaya tha
 When we hear the word Mother, the idol filled with Mamta comes in the eyes
 lekin is baat par gajiabad main rahane vaali ek maa ne kalank laga diya he
 Here a 10-year-old girl has severely accused her mother of selling her 5 times and staining her father with cigarettes and bidis
 maasoom ne bataaya, 'uski sagi maa kii maut ke baad 4 saal pehle uske 60 saal ke pita ne 21 saal kii ladki se shaadi kii
 Her step mother started harassing her since marriage
 saath hi 5 baar alag-alag logon ko bechaa

 peedit bacchee ko jaipurchild welfare cameti(seedblusi) ke madhyam se gajiabad laayaa gaya tha
 After this, the family was searched by placing him in a child home for 3 months

 He said that this is a case of child trafficking
 unhone loni thane ko letters likhakar maamle main maa or pita ke khilaaf mukadmaa darj karne kii maang kii he

 jab bacchee kaa pita bal grih se use ghar le jane ke liye pahunchaa to bacchee apane pita ko dekhakar rone lagi
 She was very scared
 poochne par usne kaha ki papa gande hai
 According to the CWC member, when the girl was questioned alone, she told the whole story
 usne bataaya ki kaise uski maa kii maut ke baad pita use pareshaan karata tha
 How did the step mother treat her
 bataaya ja rahaa he ki bacchee kii maa use apane parichit logon ke haathon bechati thi or jab isaki soochna police ko milti to vah use waapas ghar le aati thi

 com / homyb1hddi - Narendra Modi (@narendramodi) April 17, 2015 Modi's visit had a special emphasis on attracting investment and technology for the development of India through the "make in India" program
 apni germany yatra ke dauraan modi ne hanover meley kaa udghaatan kiya, jisamen bharat ek saajhedaar desh tha or iskaa shishark ‚Äò‚Äòmek in india‚Äô‚Äô rakhaa gaya tha
 The first stop of this nine-day visit to Modi was France
 paris main apane pravaas ke dauraan modi ne raashtrapati francwa oland tathaa kaarobaari netaaon se mulaakaat kii
 During this time an agreement was signed, under which India will buy 36 Rafale fighter aircraft ready to fly from France
 tippaniyan With this, it was decided to go ahead with the closed nuclear project at Jaitapur in Maharashtra
 iske baad, pradhanmantri germany gaye, jahaan unhone german chancelar anjala morkel ke saath baatcheet kii or germany se nivesh or kaarobaar ko sugam banane ke liye ek pranali bhi sthapit kiye jane kaa elaan kiya
 The two countries also agreed to expand bilateral economic cooperation
 modi kii yatra kaa antim padaav canada tha, jahaan kaarobaari netaaon se mulaakaat karne or toronto tathaa venkuvar main rukne ke saath hi unhone canada ke pradhanmantri stephen harper se otawa main mulaakaat kii
 Following this meeting, Canada agreed to supply 3,000 metric tons of uranium to India for Indian nuclear reactors from this year under a five-year deal valued at $ 254 million
 isse pehle modi ne shuukravaar ko canada kii apni yatra ke aakhri din vainkuvar pahunche or unhone yahaan ek mandir or gurudwara main jaakar mattha teka tha
 In Vancouver, PM first went to Gurdwara Khalsa Dewan and offered prayers
 is dauraan canada ke piem steefan harper bhi unke saath the
 Prime Minister Narendra Modi while addressing the people of Sikh community at the gurudwara said that he has blood relation with Sikh community
 piem ne kaha ki sikh samudaay ke log canada main kheti karne aae the, lekin aaj canada kii pahchaan main sikh samudaay ke logon kaa ahm yogadan he
 After the gurudwara, Modi also went to the Lakshmi Narayan temple, where he expressed his opinion about yoga
 piem ne yoga diwas ghoshit kiye jane par sanyukt raashtra kaa dhanyavad bhi kiya
 Earlier, inviting Canadian companies to invest in India, Prime Minister Narendra Modi told them that his government was moving fast on reforms and that it had opened up sectors like railways, insurance and housing
 modi ne guuruuvaar ko 30 sheersh companiyon ke mukhya kaaryakari adhikariyon se kaha ‚Äò‚Äòcanada main kshamta he
 India provides opportunities
 yadi donon ko mila den to aap andaja laga sakate hai ki yah sambandh kitni oonchai tak ja saktaa he
 "the Prime Minister told the ceos that there are many capabilities and opportunities in the india-canada relationship
" guuruuvaar ko pradhanmantri modi ne toronto main stephen harper ke saath air india smarak jaakar un 329 logon ko shradhanjali di, jo saal 1985 main kanishka vimaan haadase main maare gaye the
 The two Prime Ministers paid homage at the memorial and interacted with those present who lost their loved ones in that terror attack
 yah smarak saal 2007 main bana tha
 Kanishka, an Air India flight from Montreal to New Delhi, was blown up on June 23, 1985
 is aatanki hamale main 329 log maare gaye the, jinamein se adhikansh bhartiya mul ke canadai naagarik the
 The Prime Minister tweeted before his departure, "I am leaving Canada with deep satisfaction
 yah yatra bharat-canada sambandhon ko or majbootee pradaan karegi

 On Thursday, Prime Minister Modi along with Stephen Harper went to the Air India Memorial in Toronto to pay tribute to the 329 people who were killed in the Kanishka plane crash in 1985
 donon pradhanmantriyon ne smarak par shraddhasuman arpit kiye or vahaan maujuud un logon se baatcheet kii, jinhone us aatanki hamale main apane priyajanon ko kho diya

 donon deshon ne dwipaksheeya aarthik sahyog ko vistaar dene par bhi sahmati jataayi

 In order to protect the interests of domestic workers in the country, the government is formulating a national policy, which proposes to keep the minimum wage for full-time domestic help-assistants at 9,000
 iske alaava aisi gharelu naukaron ko 15 din kaa ped avkaash, maatrutiv avkaash or anya saamaajik surakshaayen praapt hongi
 The NDA government is preparing a national policy to protect the interests of domestic help-assistants, which will include all these things
 iske alaava unhen saamaajik suraksha cover bhi milegaa
 There will also be provisions for protection from sexual exploitation and bonded labor
 gharelu shramikon ke liye rashtriya niti ke masaude ko cabinet kii manjuuri ke liye jald bheja jane vaala he
 Such workers will have the right to education
 unhen surakshit kaam kaa maahaul uplabdh karaayaa jayega or ek shikaayat niptaan pranali hogi
 It also provides for compulsory contribution of the employer to the social security of the domestic workers
 aise kamgaaron ko samuhik molbhav ke liye ek-duusare se sampark karne kaa adhikaar hoga
 The Director General of Labor Welfare (DGLW) has prepared a draft that was submitted to Labor Minister Bandaru Dattatreya last week
 dattatreya ne kaha ki gharelu kaamgaar niti taiyaar kii ja rahi he, gharelu kamgaaron kaa shoshan bhi hota he aise main unka kalyaan or sangrakshan behad mahatvapurn he
 He also stated that the draft of this policy conforms to the norms of the International Samsung Organization (ILO)
 bharat ne gharelu kamgaaron ke liye ielo kii sandhi ko sweekaar kiya he
 Once this policy comes into existence, a tripartite agreement between the employer, employee and the intermediary agency connecting the two will be legally valid
 -inputbhasha Instant messaging app whatsapp is releasing a new feature
 indian yugers ko bhi ye fitures milane shuru ho gaye hai
 Earlier also we had told you about this new feature, then it was being tested
 darasal whatsapp kaa ye feechar phek news or afvaahon par lagaam lagane ke liye banaaya gaya he
 whatsapp's new feature is for the For Forwarded message
 ye feechar Android or iphone yugers ko diya jayega
 Under this feature, users will be able to know what is the frequency of getting message forward
 paanch baar se zyada kiye gaye forward massej par ye label dikhegaa
 This feature has been given in the latest version whatsapp
 whatsapp ne kaaphi pehle hi forverd kiye gaye massej par ek label kii shuruyaat kar di he
 It shows a single arrow, which means that these messages are forwarded
 ab ek nae label kii shuruyaat hui he
 It is labeled Double Arrow
 whatsapp ne kaha he ki whatsapp par Privacy or Intimacy ko menten karne ke liye company forverd massej ko limit karti he
 Message forward can only be made to five people at a time
 agar ek massej ko ek yujar paanch baar se zyada forward karata he yahaan Double Arrow kaa label banegaa
 The number of times a message is forwarded is encrypted end to end
 whatsapp ek pravaktaa ne kaha he, ‚Äòhaal hi main hamane apane forward massej label main ek apadet jari kiya he jo logon ko ye pahchaanane main madad milegi ki risive kiye gaye massej kai baar forward kiye gaye hai
 More frequently forwarded messages will be marked with double arrows and if users forward it, they will also see a notice

 The Kejriwal government refused to accept the decision of Lt
 Governor Najeeb Jung to stop the notification related to raising the circle rate on agricultural land and on Thursday directed its officials to issue an August 4 Delhi government notification on the new circle rates
 Implement nahin maanenge LG kaa aadeshisse pehle up-rajyapal ne kai khamiyaan ginate hue dilli sarkaar kii file lautaa di or phir se adhisuchana jari karne ko kaha
 The matter caught fire when it was decided in a cabinet meeting chaired by Chief Minister Arvind Kejriwal at the Delhi Secretariat that the order of the Deputy Governor would not be entertained
 'adhisuchana rokane kaa adhikaar LG ko nahin'kejariwal cabinet ne kaha ki up-rajyapal ke paas aisi kisi adhisuchana ko rokane kaa adhikaar nahin he or yah haq sirf nyaaypalika ko he
 Hours after the government's decision, the Lieutenant Governor issued a statement saying that the law was not followed in issuing the notification
 unhone sarkaar se kaha ki vah nai adhisuchana jari kare jisamen maujuuda adhisuchana kii khaamiyon ko uchit rup se sahi kiya gaya ho
 The Delhi government on Thursday passed a resolution saying that it would not follow the directions of the Lieutenant Governor related to the notification
 adhikariyon ko LG ke nirdesh na maanane kii hidaayattaaf sarkaar ne adhikariyon ko nirdesh die hai ki ve up-rajyapal ke nirdeshon kaa paalan na karen or unhen rashtriya rajdhani main krishi bhoomi ke nai sarkal daron par chaar agast kii dilli sarkaar kii adhisuchana ko lagu karnaa chahie
 Jung had withheld the government notification on August 10 raising the circle rates for agricultural land and said that the government did not take his approval
